$fun.sesp
function (thresholds, controls, cases, direction) 
{
    perf.matrix <- sapply(thresholds, roc.utils.perfs, controls = controls, 
        cases = cases, direction = direction)
    return(list(se = perf.matrix[2, ], sp = perf.matrix[1, ]))
}
